The balcony is spacious and has a clothes drying rack. The breakfast at the hotel is very rich, and the a la carte restaurant for dinner is particularly delicious. As a parent-child hotel, the children's entertainment activities are rich and attractive, and you can't finish them all if you stay for less than 3 days! Hotel guests have exclusive access to amusement parks and water parks, with unlimited entry and exit. There is also a shuttle bus to the water park, and special toiletries and bathrobes are provided for children.
It is recommended that you check in during off-peak hours, as the flow of people during peak seasons may affect your check-in experience.
Some suggestions: the buffet restaurant needs improvement, with fewer service staff and unstable food quality; the hotel is relatively large and I hope there will be clearer signage; the lockers in the water park are expensive and small and I hope they can be adjusted.
